### 1.1.3	DefineÈ™ti progresul dorit

###### ğŸ¯ Obiectiv & Scope
- **Goal:** +**10% rel.** Completion & **â‰¥70%** Final CTR prin adaptare Ã®n timp real bazatÄƒ pe **progres perceput** (*emotional / clarity / reflection / confirmation*).
- **Principii:** mÄƒsurare robustÄƒ â†’ adaptare cu **confidence + cooldown** â†’ experimentare **sequential + variance reduction** â†’ **SLO-uri**, **privacy**, **data-quality gates**, **model monitoring**.

> **CompletaÈ›i Ã®nainte de rollout:**  
> Baseline Completion: `____` â€¢ Baseline Final CTR: `____` â€¢ Baseline TTFI (median): `____` â€¢ Trafic/zi (sesiuni): `____`

---

###### ğŸ“ˆ KPI-uri & Èšinte (cu guardrails & SLO)
- **Primary:** **Quiz Completion Rate** (+10% rel. vs control).
- **Secondary:** **Final CTR** (â‰¥70% pe segmente eligibile), **TTFI median** (âˆ’15%).
- **Health:** **Î” sentiment** (QFâˆ’Q0.5) â‰¥ +0.5 (1â€“5), **TTC** â‰¤ +10%, **Abandon post-adaptare** â‰¤ +1.5pp.
- **SLO UX:** `adaptation_latency_ms P95 â‰¤ 250`, `TTI P95 â‰¤ 2.5s`, `CLS â‰¤ 0.1`.
- **SLO Date:** â‰¥**99%** evenimente cu `session_id`; â‰¤**0.5%** latenÈ›e >5s; â‰¤**0.5%** schema errors.

---

###### ğŸ§  DefiniÈ›ie OperaÈ›ionalÄƒ â€“ â€Progres perceputâ€
- **Slider 1â€“5 per Ã®ntrebare**: â€CÃ¢t te-a ajutat Ã®ntrebarea asta?â€ (1=*deloc* â€¦ 5=*mult*).
- **Momente de mÄƒsurare:** **Q3 (mid, 70% sample)** & **pre-Outro (100%)**.
- **Tip (enum):** `emotional`, `clarity`, `reflection`, `confirmation`.
- **DetecÈ›ie:** 1-tap rule-based + semnale (`time_on_question_ms`, `backtracks`, `revisions`, `free_text_len`, `sentiment_score`, `scroll_depth`).
- **Confidence:** `progress_confidence âˆˆ [0,1]`; **adaptÄƒm doar la `conf â‰¥ 0.6`**.

---

###### ğŸ”€ PoliticÄƒ de Adaptare (guardrails-first)
- **Trigger unic @Q3:** dacÄƒ `perceived_score â‰¤ 2` **sau** `delta_score â‰¤ âˆ’1`.
- **Eligibility:** min. **3 rÄƒspunsuri valide**, `bot_score â‰¤ 0.8`.
- **Cooldown:** max **1 adaptare/sesiune**. **Copy frequency cap:** â‰¤1 mesaj emoÈ›ional/sesiune.
- **Fallback:** `conf < 0.6` â†’ **`clarity_min`**.
- **Ce adaptÄƒm:** ordinea **ultimelor 2 Ã®ntrebÄƒri** + **1 bloc contextual** (validare / hint / rezumat / preview) + **micro-CTA**.
- **Ce nu adaptÄƒm:** primele **3 Ã®ntrebÄƒri** (zonÄƒ stabilÄƒ).
- **i18n & versionare:** `ro_*/en_*` Ã®n `microcopy_id`; `policy_version` Ã®n tracking.

- `emotional` â†’ validare + 1 Ã®ntrebare scurtÄƒ (â‰¤20s).  
- `clarity` â†’ hint practic + checklist 1-pas.

---

###### ğŸ§ª Plan Statistic (de elitÄƒ)
- **AA-test** *(7 zile / â‰¥5k sesiuni)*: validezi randomizare & tracking. Gate: |Î”Completion| < **1pp**, p>0.2.
- **Exposure event:** `experiment_exposure` la **eligibilitate (Q1)**, nu la `quiz_start`.
- **A/B 50/50** *(~2 sÄƒpt.)* cu **Oâ€™Brienâ€“Fleming alpha-spending** (3 looks: 25/50/100% N).
- **Variance reduction:** **CUPED** (covariate pre-tratament: `time_on_Q1_2`, `device`, `channel`).
- **Multiple testing:** **Benjaminiâ€“Hochberg** (q=0.1) pe segmente (mobile/desktop, paid/organic, new/returning).
- **Model final (readout):** logistic cu covariate; raportezi **ATE** + **heterogeneity** pe segmente.

###### ğŸ›°ï¸ Observabilitate, Privacy & Safety

- **Safety:** microcopy â€œconfirmationâ€ revizuit legal; fÄƒrÄƒ promisiuni de diagnostic.

###### ğŸ¤– Clasificator â€“ Train & Monitor

- **V1 (sÄƒpt. 3):** logistic on-device; features: `time_on_question_ms`, `revisions_count`, `free_text_len_z`, `scroll_depth_z`, `sentiment_score`.  
- **Targeturi:** **AUC â‰¥ 0.70**, **coverage (confâ‰¥0.6) 35â€“65%**, **PSI â‰¤ 0.2** (drift).

ğŸ“Š Dashboard (exec-ready)

âœ… Acceptance / No-Go

Flow: DS+PM confirmÄƒ â‰¤30m â†’ Eng OFF â†’ Decision Log + RCA 48h.

ğŸ—ºï¸ Rollout & Ramp-up (7â†’14 zile)
D1â€“D2: experiment_exposure, client_perf, alerte, AA-test ON (5%).

D3â€“D4: CUPED pipeline + contract tests (schema).

D5â€“D7: rule-based classifier & QA, Ã®nchide AA; Go/No-Go A/B.

D8: porneÈ™ti A/B 50/50 (sequential).

D9â€“D11: monitor SLO & guardrails; fixezi microcopy.

D12â€“D14: readout @50% N; decide ship/hold/kill; plan V1 ML.

Owners: PM (gates), DS (CUPED & readout), Eng (flags & perf), DX (copy & a11y).

ğŸ§· Data Quality Gates (pre-analizÄƒ)
Exclude: session_id lipsÄƒ, clock_skew_ms > 5000, bot_score > 0.8, time_on_question_ms < 300 la â‰¥2 Ã®ntrebÄƒri.

ğŸ§© Pseudocod â€” State Machine (exec)
```pesudo
onMidCheck(Q3):
  if !eligible(session) or cooldown_used: return
  if perceived_score <= 2 or (perceived_score - prev_score) <= -1:
    type, conf = detect_progress_type(features)
    branch = (conf >= 0.6) ? map(type) : "clarity_min"
    apply_adaptation(branch)
    log_adaptation(branch, policy_version="v2.4")
    cooldown_used = true
```
ğŸ§° Snippet TS/React (feature flags + Segment)
```ts
import { getFlag } from "./flags";
import analytics from "./segment";

export async function onMidCheck(ctx: Ctx) {
  if (!getFlag("adaptive_policy_v2_4_enabled")) return;
  if (ctx.qIndex !== 3 || ctx.cooldownUsed || ctx.botScore > 0.8) return;

  const { score, prevScore } = ctx.progress;
  if (score > 2 && score - prevScore > -1) return;

  const { type, conf } = await ctx.detector(ctx.features);
  const branch = conf >= 0.6 ? mapType(type) : "clarity_min";

  const t0 = performance.now();
  await ctx.applyAdaptation(branch);
  const latency = performance.now() - t0;

  analytics.track("quiz_adaptation_applied", {
    session_id: ctx.sessionId,
    branch,
    component: "order/microcopy/cta",
    policy_version: "v2.4"
  });
  analytics.track("client_perf", {
    session_id: ctx.sessionId,
    adaptation_latency_ms: Math.round(latency)
  });

  ctx.cooldownUsed = true;
}
```
ğŸ§® SQL (BigQuery) â€” Readout cu CUPED (Completion)
```sql
WITH sessions AS (
  SELECT
    session_id,
    ANY_VALUE(variant) AS variant,
    MAX(IF(event_name='quiz_complete',1,0)) AS complete,
    -- covariate pre-tratament (exposure â‰¤ Q2):
    AVG(IF(event_name='quiz_answer_submitted' AND question_number IN (1,2),
           time_on_question_ms, NULL)) AS x_cov
  FROM `proj.dataset.events`
  WHERE experiment_id = 'quiz_adaptive_v2_4'
  GROUP BY session_id
),
stats AS (
  SELECT
    VAR_POP(x_cov) AS varx,
    COVAR_POP(complete, x_cov) AS covyx
  FROM sessions
),
adjusted AS (
  SELECT
    s.*,
    -- CUPED: y' = y - Î¸(x - mean(x))
    complete - (covyx/NULLIF(varx,0)) * (x_cov - AVG(x_cov) OVER ()) AS complete_adj
  FROM sessions s CROSS JOIN stats
)
SELECT
  variant,
  AVG(complete) AS completion,
  AVG(complete_adj) AS completion_cuped,
  COUNT(*) AS n
FROM adjusted
GROUP BY variant;
```

### 1.1.4	Formulezi JTBD Ã®n stil clasic


##### ğŸ¯ Obiectiv & Scope
**MaximizÄƒm completarea È™i CTR-ul final** adaptÃ¢nd Ã®n timp real flow-ul pe baza **progresului perceput** *(emotional/clarity/reflection/confirmation)* **È™i a JTBD-ului primar detectat** *(motivaÈ›ia iniÈ›ialÄƒ)*.  
Principii: **mÄƒsurare robustÄƒ â†’ adaptare cu confidence+cooldown â†’ experimentare sequential+CUPED â†’ SLO-uri, privacy, data-quality gates, model monitoring**.

> **CompletaÈ›i Ã®nainte de rollout:**  
> Baseline Completion: `____` â€¢ Baseline Final CTR: `____` â€¢ Baseline TTFI (median): `____` â€¢ Baseline JTBD Satisfaction: `____` â€¢ Trafic/zi: `____`

---

##### ğŸ“ˆ KPI-uri & Èšinte (combinat Progres + JTBD)
- **Primary:** **Quiz Completion Rate** **+10% rel.** vs control (ex: 55%â†’60.5%).
- **Secondary:** **Final CTR** â‰¥ **70%**; **TTFI median** âˆ’**15%**; **JTBD Satisfaction Rate** (self_reported_value â‰¥4/5) â‰¥ **75%**.
- **Health/Guardrails:** Abandon post-adaptare â‰¤ **+1.5pp**; **TTC** â‰¤ **+10%**; **Î” sentiment** (QFâˆ’Q0.5) â‰¥ **+0.5**.
- **SLO UX:** `adaptation_latency_ms P95 â‰¤ 250`, `TTI P95 â‰¤ 2.5s`, `CLS â‰¤ 0.1`.  
- **SLO Date:** â‰¥**99%** evenimente cu `session_id`; â‰¤**0.5%** schema errors/late >5s.

---

##### ğŸ§  DefiniÈ›ii OperaÈ›ionale

###### A) Progres perceput
- **Slider 1â€“5 per Ã®ntrebare:** â€CÃ¢t te-a ajutat Ã®ntrebarea asta?â€
- **Momente:** **Q3 (mid, 70% sample)** È™i **pre-Outro (100%)**.
- **Tipuri:** `emotional`, `clarity`, `reflection`, `confirmation`.
- **Semnale implicite:** `time_on_question_ms`, `backtracks`, `revisions`, `free_text_len`, `sentiment_score`, `scroll_depth`.
- **Confidence:** `progress_confidence âˆˆ [0,1]`; adaptÄƒm doar dacÄƒ **conf â‰¥ 0.6**.

###### B) JTBD primar
- **DetecÈ›ie @Q0â€“Q1 (Ã®nainte de primele 3 Ã®ntrebÄƒri):**
  - **1 Ã®ntrebare rapidÄƒ** (single-select) + opÈ›ional 1 free-text scurt *(â‰¤80c)*.
  - **Enum:** `emo_support`, `action_now`, `social_confirmation`, `resource_discovery`.
  - **Semnale auxiliare:** sursÄƒ trafic, cuvinte cheie free-text, `time_to_first_click`.
- **Confidence:** `jtbd_confidence âˆˆ [0,1]`; dacÄƒ **<0.6** â†’ default `action_now`.
- **SatisfaÈ›ie JTBD:** QF â€Ai obÈ›inut ce cÄƒutai?â€ (1â€“5).

---

##### ğŸ”€ PoliticÄƒ de Adaptare (2D Matrix, guardrails-first)
- **Trigger unic @Q3:** `perceived_score â‰¤ 2` **sau** `delta_score â‰¤ âˆ’1`.
- **Eligibility:** min **3 rÄƒspunsuri valide**, `bot_score â‰¤ 0.8`.
- **Cooldown:** max **1 adaptare/sesiune**. **Frequency cap:** â‰¤1 mesaj emoÈ›ional/sesiune.
- **Fallback:** dacÄƒ `progress_conf<0.6` â†’ `clarity_min`; dacÄƒ `jtbd_conf<0.6` â†’ tratezi `jtbd='action_now'`.
- **Ce adaptÄƒm:** ordinea **ultimelor 2 Ã®ntrebÄƒri** + **1 bloc contextual** + **micro-CTA**.  
- **Ce nu adaptÄƒm:** primele **3 Ã®ntrebÄƒri** (zonÄƒ stabilÄƒ).  
- **i18n & versionare:** `ro_*/en_*` Ã®n `microcopy_id`; `policy_version="v3.0"` Ã®n tracking.

###### Decizie 2D `(progress_type, jtbd_primary) â†’ branch_id`
| progress \ jtbd | emo_support | action_now | social_confirmation | resource_discovery |
|---|---:|---:|---:|---:|
| emotional | `branch_emo_relief` | `branch_emoâ†’clarity_bridge` | `branch_social_valid` | `branch_emo_res_preview` |
| clarity | `branch_clarity_checklist` | `branch_clarity_one_step` | `branch_clarity_norms` | `branch_clarity_resources` |
| reflection | `branch_reflect_summary` | `branch_reflectâ†’action` | `branch_reflect_social` | `branch_reflect_resources` |
| confirmation | `branch_confirm_preview` | `branch_confirmâ†’step` | `branch_confirm_social` | `branch_confirm_resources` |

> **Principiu:** dacÄƒ existÄƒ conflict, *JTBD dicteazÄƒ tipul CTA*, iar *progress_type dicteazÄƒ microcopy-ul*.

---

##### ğŸ¤– Pseudocod â€” State Machine (JTBD + Progres)
```pseudo
init @Q0:
  jtbd, jtbd_conf = detect_jtbd(signals)
  if jtbd_conf < 0.6: jtbd = "action_now"

onMidCheck @Q3:
  if !eligible(session) or cooldown_used: return
  if perceived_score <= 2 or (perceived_score - prev_score) <= -1:
    ptype, pconf = detect_progress_type(features)
    branch = (pconf >= 0.6) ? MATRIX[ptype][jtbd] : "clarity_min"
    apply_adaptation(branch); log_adaptation(branch, policy_version="v3.0")
    cooldown_used = true
beforeOutro:
  personalize_outro(dominant_progress(), jtbd)
```

###### ğŸ§ª Plan Statistic (de elitÄƒ)
AA-test (7 zile / â‰¥5k sesiuni): randomizare + tracking OK. Gate: |Î”Completion|<1pp, p>0.2.

Exposure event: experiment_exposure la eligibilitate (Q1).

A/B 50/50 (â‰ˆ2 sÄƒpt.) cu Oâ€™Brienâ€“Fleming alpha-spending (looks: 25/50/100% N).

Variance reduction: CUPED (covariate pre-tratament: time_on_Q1_2, device, channel).

Multiple testing: Benjaminiâ€“Hochberg (q=0.1) pe segmente (mobile/desktop, paid/organic, new/returning).

Readout: logistic cu covariate; raportezi ATE + heterogeneity pe (jtbd_primary, progress_type).

###### ğŸ›°ï¸ Observabilitate, Privacy & Safety
Alerting: Î”Completion adaptiveâ€“control < âˆ’2pp/60m â†’ page PM+Eng; adaptation_latency_ms P95 > 250 Ã®n 3/5 batch-uri â†’ auto-degrade la static.

Privacy/Consent: consent_update (required/optional/none), age_bucket; user_id hash; retention 90/365 zile.

Safety: copy de confirmation QA legal; fÄƒrÄƒ promisiuni de diagnostic.

###### ğŸ¤– Clasificatoare â€” Train & Monitor
JTBD V0: rule-based + keyword list; V1 (sÄƒpt.3): logistic multi-class (on-device).

Progres V0: rule-based; V1: logistic (features timp/scroll/sentiment).

Targets: AUC â‰¥ 0.70 / F1 macro â‰¥ 0.65; coverage confâ‰¥0.6 Ã®ntre 35â€“65%; PSI â‰¤ 0.2.

Fail-safe: dacÄƒ AUC<0.65 24h â†’ branch=clarity_min (forÈ›at).

###### ğŸ§® SQL â€” Readout JTBD Satisfaction & Heterogeneity

```sql
WITH sess AS (
  SELECT
    session_id,
    ANY_VALUE(variant) AS variant,
    ANY_VALUE(jtbd_primary) AS jtbd,
    MAX(IF(event_name='quiz_complete',1,0)) AS complete,
    MAX(IF(event_name='quiz_cta_clicked',1,0)) AS cta_click,
    MAX(IF(event_name='jtbd_satisfied', self_reported_value, NULL)) AS jtbd_value
  FROM `proj.dataset.events`
  WHERE experiment_id = 'quiz_adaptive_v3_0'
  GROUP BY session_id
)
SELECT
  variant, jtbd,
  AVG(complete) AS completion,
  AVG(cta_click) AS ctr_final,
  AVG(IF(jtbd_value>=4,1,0)) AS jtbd_satisfaction_rate,
  COUNT(*) AS n
FROM sess
GROUP BY variant, jtbd
ORDER BY jtbd, variant;
```
###### ğŸ§° Snippet TS/React â€” JTBD + Progres

```ts
export async function onStart(ctx: Ctx) {
  const { jtbd, conf } = await ctx.detectJTBD(ctx.signalsQ0);
  ctx.traits.jtbdPrimary = conf >= 0.6 ? jtbd : "action_now";
  analytics.track("jtbd_detected", {
    session_id: ctx.sessionId,
    jtbd_primary: ctx.traits.jtbdPrimary,
    jtbd_confidence: conf,
    policy_version: "v3.0"
  });
}

export async function onMidCheck(ctx: Ctx) {
  if (!flags.enabled("adaptive_policy_v3_0_enabled")) return;
  if (ctx.qIndex !== 3 || ctx.cooldownUsed || ctx.botScore > 0.8) return;

  const { score, prevScore } = ctx.progress;
  if (score > 2 && score - prevScore > -1) return;

  const { type, conf } = await ctx.detectProgress(ctx.features);
  const ptype = conf >= 0.6 ? type : "clarity";
  const branch = MATRIX[ptype][ctx.traits.jtbdPrimary] || "clarity_min";

  const t0 = performance.now();
  await ctx.applyAdaptation(branch);
  analytics.track("quiz_adaptation_applied", {
    session_id: ctx.sessionId, branch, component: "order/microcopy/cta", policy_version: "v3.0"
  });
  analytics.track("client_perf", {
    session_id: ctx.sessionId, adaptation_latency_ms: Math.round(performance.now() - t0)
  });
  ctx.cooldownUsed = true;
}
```

### 1.1.5	Distingi Ã®ntre JTBD funcÈ›ional È™i emoÈ›ional
### 1.1.5 Distingi Ã®ntre JTBD funcÈ›ional È™i emoÈ›ional

**DefiniÈ›ie:**
- **JTBD FuncÈ›ional** â€” job-ul principal al utilizatorului exprimat Ã®n termeni de *task concret* sau *rezultat tangibil* pe care vrea sÄƒ-l obÈ›inÄƒ.  
  â†’ Exemplu: â€SÄƒ gÄƒsesc un pas clar pe care sÄƒ-l fac Ã®n seara asta cu copilulâ€  
- **JTBD EmoÈ›ional** â€” job-ul principal exprimat Ã®n termeni de *stare doritÄƒ*, *trÄƒire* sau *nevoie de validare*.  
  â†’ Exemplu: â€SÄƒ mÄƒ simt Ã®nÈ›eles(Äƒ) È™i mai liniÈ™tit(Äƒ) dupÄƒ o zi greaâ€

---

**Ãn quiz-ul adaptiv Progres + JTBD:**
- **DetecÈ›ie JTBD funcÈ›ional:**  
  - Cuvinte-cheie orientate spre acÈ›iune (â€œvreau sÄƒ facâ€¦â€, â€œcum pot sÄƒâ€¦â€).  
  - JTBD-uri standard: `action_now`, `resource_discovery`.  
  - Semnale implicite: rÄƒspunsuri concise, alegere rapidÄƒ a opÈ›iunilor practice, TTI (Time to Interaction) scÄƒzut.
- **DetecÈ›ie JTBD emoÈ›ional:**  
  - Cuvinte-cheie de stare (â€œvreau sÄƒ mÄƒ simtâ€¦â€, â€œam nevoie sÄƒâ€¦â€).  
  - JTBD-uri standard: `emo_support`, `social_confirmation`.  
  - Semnale implicite: timp mai mare pe prima Ã®ntrebare, free-text lung, menÈ›iuni de sentimente.

---

**MatricÄƒ de adaptare:**
| JTBD Tip | Exemple tipice | ImplicaÈ›ie UX | Microcopy dominant |
|---|---|---|---|
| FuncÈ›ional | action_now, resource_discovery | CTA-uri clare, paÈ™i concreÈ›i, liste | â€ÃncearcÄƒ asta disearÄƒ: [pas]â€ |
| EmoÈ›ional | emo_support, social_confirmation | Validare, ton empatic, reducere presiune | â€E Ã®n regulÄƒ sÄƒ fie greu. MulÈ›i pÄƒrinÈ›i simt la fel.â€ |

---

**Guardrails:**
- Nu amesteca mesajele funcÈ›ionale cu cele emoÈ›ionale Ã®n acelaÈ™i bloc de adaptare â€” creeazÄƒ disonanÈ›Äƒ.
- DacÄƒ clasificatorul nu depÄƒÈ™eÈ™te **conf â‰¥0.6**, foloseÈ™te fallback la `action_now` (funcÈ›ional) pentru a pÄƒstra claritatea.

---

**Tracking adiÈ›ional:**
- `jtbd_type` (enum: functional/emotional) derivat din `jtbd_primary`.
- Permite analize comparative: **Completion** È™i **CTR** pe tip JTBD, plus corelaÈ›ia cu `progress_type_detected`.

---

**KPIs specifice:**
- **FuncÈ›ional:** % utilizatori care raporteazÄƒ â€Am obÈ›inut un pas concretâ€ â‰¥ **80%** Ã®n `jtbd_satisfied`.
- **EmoÈ›ional:** % utilizatori care raporteazÄƒ â€M-am simÈ›it Ã®nÈ›eles(Äƒ)â€ â‰¥ **80%**.

---

**TL;DR:**  
SeparÄƒ JTBD Ã®n *funcÈ›ional* È™i *emoÈ›ional* pentru adaptare mai precisÄƒ, evitÃ¢nd mesaje mixte È™i mÄƒsurÃ¢nd satisfacÈ›ia per categorie.

### 1.1.6	Mapezi JTBD la flow-ul actual

### 1.1.6 Mapezi JTBD la flow-ul actual

**Scop:**  
Asiguri coerenÈ›a dintre JTBD-urile detectate È™i structura actualÄƒ a quiz-ului (ordinea Ã®ntrebÄƒrilor, tipul de conÈ›inut, tonul microcopy È™i CTA-uri) astfel Ã®ncÃ¢t utilizatorul sÄƒ simtÄƒ progres relevant faÈ›Äƒ de *job-ul* sÄƒu iniÈ›ial.

---

#### 1) Inventarierea flow-ului actual
**Exemplu (flow v2.4):**
1. **Q0â€“Q1:** intro + Ã®ntrebare iniÈ›ialÄƒ (detectare JTBD)  
2. **Q2:** Ã®ntrebare de context (stare/obiceiuri)  
3. **Q3:** Ã®ntrebare pivot (mid-check progres perceput)  
4. **Q4â€“Q5:** Ã®ntrebÄƒri finale (detalii specifice / validare)  
5. **Outro:** rezultat + CTA principal

---

#### 2) Maparea JTBD â†’ elemente flow

3.3 ğŸ”¬ Variabile derivate (computed, low-cost)

## **8. Verifici flow logic & UX**

8.1 ğŸ—ºï¸ Harta de flow (state machine, MVP)

8.2 âœ… Acceptance (logic & UX) â€” checklist scurt

10.7 ğŸ¤– LogicÄƒ adaptivÄƒ â€” state machine (MVP)
pseudo
Copy
Edit
on Q0.5 (70% sample):
  if perceived_progress_score <= 2:
     intent_profile, intent_confidence = infer_intent(Q1..Q2 features)
     if intent_confidence >= 0.6 and !cooldown_used:
        apply(branch_for[intent_profile])   # Norman / Torres / Neutral
        cooldown_used = true                # max 1 adaptare
     else:
        apply("Clarity_min")                # fallback determinist
before Outro:
  personalize outro by (intent_profile Â± baby_wording if Q2<2y)

10.9 ğŸ“ˆ Tracking â€” tracking.yaml (MVP PostHogâ†’GA4)
yaml
Copy
Edit
events:
  - name: quiz_intro_shown
    props: [session_id, variant, device, net_type, ts]
  - name: quiz_start_clicked
    props: [session_id, copy_id, ts]
  - name: quiz_question_shown
    props: [session_id, question_id, order, microcopy_id, question_text_len, options_count]
  - name: quiz_answer_submitted
    props: [session_id, question_id, time_on_question_ms, backtracked, tap_errors, chosen_option_id, chosen_option_tags]
  - name: quiz_intent_inferred
    props: [session_id, intent_profile, intent_confidence, features_used]
  - name: quiz_progress_update
    props: [session_id, question_number, perceived_progress_score, progress_type_detected, branch_used]
  - name: quiz_adaptation_triggered
    props: [session_id, reason, branch_applied, cooldown_active]
  - name: quiz_complete
    props: [session_id, final_progress_type, completion_time_sec, user_sentiment_post_quiz, progress_delta]
  - name: quiz_cta_clicked
    props: [session_id, cta_id, cta_label, cta_position, copy_id, ts]
  - name: calm_tip_open
    props: [session_id, tip_id, ts]
metrics:
  completion_rate: "count(quiz_complete) / count(quiz_intro_shown)"
  final_ctr_outro: "count(quiz_cta_clicked where cta_position='outro') / count(quiz_complete)"
  activation_rate: "count(calm_tip_open within 120s of quiz_cta_clicked) / count(quiz_complete)"
  ttv_tip_median_sec: "median(calm_tip_open.ts - quiz_cta_clicked.ts)"
guardrails:
  lcp_p75_ms: "<=2500"
  feedback_p95_ms: "<=1500"
  tap_error_rate: "<=0.01"
10.10 ğŸš¦ Rollout & Go/No-Go

No-Go: orice 2 guardrails Ã®ncÄƒlcate 2h consecutiv â†’ kill-switch (quiz_adaptive_enabled=false, branch Clarity_min).
